     <div data-vg="mwf-banner-VG5" data-grid="container">
      <div data-grid="col-6" class="m-banner x-type-">
       <picture></picture>
       <h2 class="c-heading-2">Xbox app</h2>
      </div>
     </div>
    </section>
    <section id="games_pivot-2" role="tabpanel" aria-label="pivot panel of Stay connected,Find new gamers, In-home streaming and Follow PC Games">
     <div data-grid="container" data-vg="mwf-pivot-multifeature-VG2">
      <div data-grid="col-12 stack-2" class="m-multi-feature f-align-center">
       <section>
        <div class="c-pivot">
         <button class="c-flipper f-previous" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></button>
         <div role="tablist">
          <a class="f-active" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-controls="newRTBItemImage11 newRTBItemContent11">Stay connected</a>
          <a role="tab" aria-controls="newRTBItemImage12 newRTBItemContent12">Find new gamers</a>
          <a role="tab" aria-controls="newRTBItemImage13 newRTBItemContent13">In-home streaming</a>
          <a role="tab" aria-controls="newRTBItemImage14 newRTBItemContent14">Follow PC Games</a>
         </div>
         <button class="c-flipper f-next" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></button>
         <section id="newRTBItemContent11" role="tabpanel" aria-hidden="false">
          <p class="c-paragraph-3">The Xbox app brings together your friends, games, and accomplishments across Xbox One, Windows 10, iOS, and Android devices. Stay connected to your Xbox Live community, join Clubs, find gamers to play with using Looking for Group, and record your epic gaming moments with Game DVR.<sup>5</sup></p>
         </section>
         <section id="newRTBItemContent12" role="tabpanel" aria-hidden="true">
          <p class="c-paragraph-3">Finding gamers has never been easier. With new features like Looking for Group and Clubs on Xbox Live, you can seek out players for your favorite games and join communities of gamers based on your interests.</p>
         </section>
         <section id="newRTBItemContent13" role="tabpanel" aria-hidden="true">
          <p class="c-paragraph-3">Stream games from your Xbox One to any Windows 10 PC at home, including your Xbox 360 games via Backward Compatibility. And now you can even stream Xbox One games directly to your Oculus Rift headset. Just connect to your console via the Xbox One Streaming app and watch your games come to life on a huge virtual screen in three immersive virtual theaters.<sup>6</sup></p>
         </section>
         <section id="newRTBItemContent14" role="tabpanel" aria-hidden="true">
          <p class="c-paragraph-3">Now the top PC games will start showing up on Xbox Live. See what your friends are playing, share and watch game clips, and access Game Hubs for your favorite PC titles.</p>
         </section>
        </div>
